<section class="main__section main__section--default aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="main__section--wrapper main__section--color main__section--color-white" v-if="validateDigitalRule('')">
<div class="main__section--wrapper-container">
<div class="row section__container__row">
<div class="col section__container__col">
<article class="responsivegrid">
<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12">
<div class="cmp-sectioncontent aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text cmp__richtext--color cmp__richtext--color-null" v-if="validateDigitalRule('')">
<h2 style="text-align: center;">Privacy Notice</h2>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cmp-divider aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><hr/></div>
<div class="richtext text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text cmp__richtext--color cmp__richtext--color-default" v-if="validateDigitalRule('')">
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Effective date: December 01, 2021</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">This Notice provides information about data we collect, use, and share, and our commitment to using the personal data we collect in a respectful fashion.</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#information">What Kinds of Information Do We Collect?</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#how">How Do We Use the Information We Collect?</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#third">Third-Party Advertising</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#who">Who Do We Share Personal Data With?</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#security">How Do We Protect Your Data?</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#choices">What Choices Do You Have About Your Personal Data?</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#retain">How Long Does McAfee Retain the Personal Data it Collects?</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#childrens">Children's Privacy</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#eea">Residents of the EEA</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#authority">Supervisory authority and complaints</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#japan">Residents of Japan, Argentina, and Canada</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#california">Residents of California</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#nevada">Residents of Nevada</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#personalinfo">Public Notice for Transfer of Personal Information </a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#links">Links to other websites</a></span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a href="#contact">Contact Us</a></span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We at McAfee, LLC, including our affiliates (“McAfee”, “we”, “us”, “our”), care deeply about privacy, security, and online safety, all of which are a significant part of our essential mission: to protect users of our products and services (“you” and “your”) from the risks of theft, disruption, and unauthorized access to their online information and activities. This Privacy Notice (“Notice”) is designed to inform you about how we collect, use, and share your personal data through our website (our “Site”), products, services, and web-based and mobile applications (collectively, the “Services”) or when you interact with us.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">McAfee sells products and services directly to consumers (you can find more information about those products here, “<a href="/en-us/consumer-products.html" target="_blank"><u>Consumer Products</u></a>”). This Privacy Notice applies both to the information we collect from you or your device when you download one of our Services and to the information we collect when one of our distribution partners installs our Services on your device.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">When you access or use our Services, you acknowledge that you have read this Notice and understand its contents. Your use of our Services and the Site and any dispute over privacy is subject to this Notice, any applicable Terms of Service (including any applicable limitations on damages and the resolution of disputes) and any applicable End User License Agreement.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">As McAfee grows, our business changes, and we may update this Notice at any time as we deem appropriate to reflect those changes. If there are any material changes to this Privacy Notice, we will notify you by email, in-product notification, or as otherwise required by applicable law. It is important that you check back and make sure that you have reviewed the most current version of this Notice.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">This Notice applies to all users of our Services across the world. Some users, including residents of the European Economic Area, may have additional rights depending on where they are located, which are described in this Notice.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="information"></a>What Kinds of Information Do We Collect?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">In order to provide our services, we collect information. Some information you provide directly to us, some we collect automatically through our Services, and some is collected from third parties. In this Notice, "Personal Data" refers to data that could be used, alone or in combination with other data, to identify you as an individual.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>We collect information you provide to us</b>. For example, we collect information when you purchase a product or service, create an account, fill out a form, participate in a contest or promotion, request customer service, or otherwise communicate with us.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">The types of Personal Data you may provide includes:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Contact information (such as name, email address, mailing address, and phone number)</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Payment information (including payment card numbers and associated identifiers, billing address, and bank account information); and</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Account log-in credentials (which for some Services may include social network credentials).</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We may also collect other information from or about you, such as information about what products you purchased, your interests, demographic information, photographs and videos, and biometric data such as fingerprints or voice prints. You may also provide us with additional data. For example, when you use our identity monitoring services, you will have the option to provide your social media log-in information so that we can monitor your social media accounts.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>We automatically collect information about your interactions with the Services as well as devices on which the Services are installed. In some cases, we automatically collect information about other devices connected to the same network as the device on which the Services are installed.</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">For example, we may collect and use the following:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Information about the products you looked at or searched for and the Services you used, including time spent and other statistical information.</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Details about your computers, devices, applications, and networks, including internet protocol (IP) address, cookie identifiers, mobile carrier, Bluetooth device IDs, mobile device ID, mobile advertising identifiers, MAC address, IMEI, Advertiser IDs, and other device identifiers that are automatically assigned to your computer or device when you access the Internet, browser type and language, language preferences, battery level, on/off status, geo-location information, hardware type, operating system, Internet service provider, pages that you visit before and after using the Services, the date and time of your visit, the amount of time you spend on each page, information about the links you click and pages you view within the Services, and other actions taken through use of the Services such as preferences. We may collect this information through our Services or through other methods of web analysis.</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">When you use our products to protect your mobile device, we collect geolocation data of the device on which the product is installed.</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Details about your internet, app, or network usage (including URLs or domain names of websites you visit, information about the applications installed on your device, or traffic data); and performance information, crash logs, and other aggregate or statistical information.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">In order to provide you our Services, including to detect and evaluate malware and spam, we may scan, collect, and store data from your files, including emails, attachments, email addresses, metadata, and URLs and traffic data.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We collect this information through our Services and through technologies such as cookies, web beacons or web bugs, and clear GIFs. Please see our <a href="#cookie" target="_blank"><u>Cookie Notice</u></a> for more information about the cookies and similar technologies that we use and the choices available to you.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Note that if you use our VPN services, our VPN servers do not look at or log any information that you send or receive on the internet.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Information We Collect from Third Parties</b><br/>
 We may receive information about you from other sources and combine that information with the information we collect directly. Examples of information we may receive from other sources include: updated delivery or payment information used to correct our records; purchase or redemption information; and customer support and enrolment information. For our identity protection Consumer Products, we also may collect credit or identity information which we use to help prevent and detect fraud.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Location Information</b><br/>
 Certain Services may request permission to access your location. Where you grant this permission, we will collect information about your location using GPS, wireless, or Bluetooth technology. You can control access to precise location information through your mobile device settings. We also may look up your IP address to determine your general location.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="how"></a>How Do We Use the Information We Collect?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>To Help Protect You</b><br/>
 When you install or use one of our Services, it will run in the background of your device or environment to help predict threats and better protect you, your devices, and your information. For example, McAfee may use information to:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Analyze data sent to/from your device(s) to isolate and identify threats, vulnerabilities, viruses, suspicious activity, spam, and attacks, and communicate with you about potential threats;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Participate in threat intelligence networks, conduct research, and adapt products and services to help respond to new threats;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Encrypt your data, lockdown a device, or back-up or recover your data;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Check for Service updates and create performance reports on our Services, to ensure they are performing properly; and</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Look for misuses of your data when you use our identity monitoring products.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>To Run Our Business<br/>
</b>We also use the information we collect for other business purposes, including to:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Authenticate your identity and prevent fraud with your biometric data;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Analyze your behavior to measure, customize, and improve our Site and Services, including developing new products and services;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Advertise McAfee products and services that we think may be of interest to you;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Establish and manage accounts and licenses, including by collecting and processing payments and completing transactions;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Provide customer support, troubleshoot issues, manage subscriptions, and respond to requests, questions, and comments;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Communicate about, and administer participation in, special events, programs, surveys, contests, sweepstakes, and other offers and promotions;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Conduct market and consumer research and trend analyses;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Enable posting on our blogs, forums, and other public communications;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Perform accounting, auditing, billing, reconciliation, and collection activities;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Prevent, detect, identify, investigate, and respond to potential or actual claims, liabilities, prohibited behavior, and criminal activity; and</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Comply with and enforce legal rights, requirements, agreements, and policies.</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Cookies are used to record your interactions with our Site.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="third"></a>Third-Party Advertising</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We work with third-party advertising companies to display or deliver ads to you while you are on our Site or using some Services. These third-party advertisers may collect data about your interaction with the Site or Services or others’ sites or services to measure the effectiveness of their ads and to personalize advertising content. See our <a href="#cookie" target="_blank"><u>Cookie Notice</u></a> to learn more about how McAfee and these advertising partners use tracking technologies like cookies and the choices available to you.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you have consented to allow our Services to access to your location, our mobile advertising partners may use your location to target advertisements to you. You may use the location settings on your device to withdraw access to information about your location</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Other Uses<br/>
</b>We may use Personal Data for which we have a legitimate interest, such as direct marketing, individual or market research, anti-fraud protection, or any other purpose disclosed to you at the time you provide Personal Data or with your consent.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="who"></a>Who Do We Share Personal Data With?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Generally, we disclose the information we collect to provide the Services, to communicate with you, to advertise or promote our Services, to facilitate changes to or transfers of our business, as required by law, or with your consent. We may share Personal information in the following ways:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">With current and future members of the McAfee family of companies for the purposes described in this Notice;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">With service providers who perform services for us (see the list of our sub-processors for <u><a href="/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html" target="_blank">Consumer Products</a></u> is available upon request for where required under applicable laws)</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If we believe disclosure is necessary and appropriate to prevent physical, financial, or other harm, injury, or loss, including to protect against fraud or credit risk;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">To legal, governmental, or judicial authorities as instructed or required by those authorities and applicable laws, or in relation to a legal activity, such as in response to a subpoena or investigation of suspected illicit or illegal activities, or where we believe in good faith that users may be engaged in illicit or illegal activities, or where we are bound by contract or law to enable a customer or business partner to comply with applicable laws;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">In connection with, or during negotiations for, an acquisition, merger, asset sale, or other similar business transfer that involves all or substantially all of our assets or functions where Personal Data is transferred or shared as part of the business assets (provided that such party agrees to use or disclose such Personal Data consistent with this Notice or gains your consent for other uses or disclosures);</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">With your consent or at your direction, such as when you choose to share information or publicly post content and reviews (for example, social media posts); and</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">With persons of your choosing and at your discretion, should the product you are subscribed to allow that functionality.</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We may also share aggregate data that does not identify you or any specific device with third parties.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="security"></a>How Do We Protect Your Data?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We use administrative, organizational, technical, and physical safeguards to protect the Personal Data we collect and process. Our security controls are designed to maintain data confidentiality, integrity, and an appropriate level of availability.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="choices"></a>What Choices Do You Have About Your Personal Data?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>McAfee Accounts</b><br/>
 If you register a McAfee Consumer Product, you can access and correct the Personal Data in your profile at any time by visiting <a href="https://home.mcafee.com/Secure/MyAccount/DashBoard.aspx?culture=en-us" target="_blank"><u>My Account</u></a> or contacting us as described below.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you have not registered a McAfee product but one of our products is installed on your device, you may stop McAfee’s collection of Personal data from your device by uninstalling that product.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">To close your account and for other support questions, please visit the McAfee <a href="https://service.mcafee.com" target="_blank"><u>Contact Us</u></a> page and click on “Support” tab and then select your "Country".</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Marketing Communications<br/>
</b>To stop receiving marketing communications, click on the unsubscribe link in the email, or click <a href="https://home.mcafee.com/supportpages/unsub.aspx" target="_blank"><u>here</u></a> for Consumer marketing.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you choose to no longer receive marketing information, McAfee may still communicate with you regarding transactional, legal or administrative topics, such as security updates, product functionality, and service requests.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><span><b>Individual Rights in Personal Data</b><br/>
 In accordance with applicable law, you may have the right to: (i) request confirmation of whether we are processing your Personal Data; (ii) obtain access to or a copy of your Personal Data; (iii) receive a portable copy of your Personal Data, or ask us to send that information to another organization (the “right of data portability”); (iv) seek correction or amendment of inaccurate, untrue, incomplete, or improperly processed Personal Data; (v) restrict our processing of your Personal Data; (vi) object to our processing of your Personal Data; and (vii) request erasure of Personal Data held about you by us, subject to certain exceptions prescribed by law.</span></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you would like to exercise any of these rights, please visit our Individual Data Request Form available at <a href="/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html">https://www.mcafee.com/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html</a> or contact us as set forth below. We will process such requests in accordance with applicable laws. To protect your privacy, we may take steps to verify your identity before fulfilling your request. For some requests and where permitted by law, an administrative fee may be charged. We will advise you of any applicable fee prior to performing your request.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="retain"></a>How Long Does McAfee Retain the Personal Data it Collects?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">McAfee will keep your Personal Data for the minimum period necessary for the purposes set out in this Notice, namely (i) for as long as you are a registered subscriber or user of our products or (ii) for as long as your Personal Data are necessary in connection with the lawful purposes set out in this Notice, for which we have a valid legal basis or (iii) for as long as is reasonably necessary for business purposes related to provision of the Services, such as internal reporting and reconcil-iation purposes, warranties or to provide you with feedback or information you might request. Where required by law, we will delete your biometric data within three years of your last interac-tion with the Services.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">In addition, if any relevant legal claims are brought, we may continue to process your Personal Data for such additional periods as are necessary in connection with that claim.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Once the abovementioned periods, each to the extent applicable, have concluded, we will either permanently delete, destroy, or de-identify the relevant Personal Data so that it can no longer reasonably be tied to you.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="childrens"></a>Children's Privacy</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Some of McAfee’s Services provide security features that parents may use to monitor their child’s activity online, physical location, or use of a registered device. These Services require parental consent, and we do not knowingly use the Personal Data we collect from children’s devices for any purpose except to deliver the Services. These products allow parents to delete their child’s profile at any time. If you believe we have collected information from your child in error or have questions or concerns about our practices relating to children, please contact us as described be-low. If you are under the age of 18, you must have your parent’s permission to access the Ser-vices. McAfee urges parents to instruct their children never to give out their real names, address-es, or phone numbers, without parental permission. If you learn that your child has provided us with Personal Data without your consent, you may alert us by contacting us as described below. If we learn that we have collected any Personal Data from children under 13 (and in certain jurisdic-tions under the age of 16), we will promptly take steps to delete such information and terminate the child’s account.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Data Transfers</b><br/>
 McAfee is headquartered in the United States (see Contact Us for addresses), and we have operations, entities, and service providers in the United States and throughout the world. As such, we and our service providers may transfer your Personal Data to, or store or access it in, jurisdictions that may not provide equivalent levels of data protection as your home jurisdiction. We will take steps to ensure that your Personal Data receives an adequate level of protection in the jurisdictions in which we process it.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="eea"></a>Residents of the European Economic Area</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you are in the European Economic (EEA), the following additional disclosures apply.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Data Controller</b><br/>
 Where you purchase one of McAfee’s consumer products, McAfee Ireland Limited acts as the Controller of your Personal Data.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Legal Basis for Processing</b><br/>
 When we process your Personal Data, we will only do so in the following situations:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We need to use your Personal Data to perform our responsibilities under our contract with you (e.g. processing payments for and providing the Services you purchase or request).</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We have a legitimate interest in processing your Personal Data. For example, we have a legitimate interest in processing your Personal Data to provide, secure, and improve our Services, in communicating with you about changes to our Services, and in informing you about new services or products.</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We have your consent to do so.</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We need to process your Personal Data to comply with our legal obligations.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Data Transfers</b><br/>
 We transfer Personal Data to countries outside of the EEA or Switzerland through a series of intercompany agreements based on the Standard Contractual Clauses in accordance with EU law and applicable EU regulations.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Individual Rights Requests and Withdraw Consent</b><br/>
 You may submit a request to exercise your rights in Personal Data using the mechanisms explained under "What Choices Do You Have About Your Personal Data?" above. If you initially consented to our processing of your Personal Data, you may withdraw your consent using those mechanisms or by contacting us using the contact information below.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="authority"></a>Supervisory Authority and Complaints</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you are an EU/EEA Data Subject and have a concern about our practices concerning the processing of Personal Data that we are not able to resolve, you have the right to lodge a complaint with the data protection authority where you reside or in which you work, or in which the alleged infringement occurred, each as applicable, or by contacting the Irish supervisory authority for data protection issues, at <a href="https://www.dataprotection.ie/docs/Home/4.htm">https://www.dataprotection.ie/docs/Home/4.htm</a>, or +353 57 868 4800.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="japan"></a>Residents of Japan, Argentina, and Canada</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you are a resident of Japan, Argentina, or Canada and you have an inquiry regarding your personal information held by McAfee, including your personal information collected through your use of our products you may request further information using the Individual Data Request Form available at <a href="/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html">https://www.mcafee.com/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html</a>.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="california"></a>Residents of California</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Your California Privacy Rights - Shine the Light Law</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">McAfee does not share information that identifies you personally with non-affiliated third parties for their own marketing use without your permission.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a><b>California Consumer Privacy Act</b></a></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you are a resident of California, you may submit a request to exercise your rights in Personal Data using the Individual Data Request Form available at <a href="/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html">https://www.mcafee.com/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html</a> For purposes of the California Consumer Privacy Act, McAfee does not “sell” your Personal Data.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="nevada"></a>Residents of Nevada</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">McAfee does not sell information that identifies you personally with non-affiliated third parties. If you would like to make a request that we not sell identifying information about you in the future, you may make a request using the contact information below.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="personalinfo"></a>Public Notice for Transfer of Personal Information</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">The assets and employees of McAfee Korea Limited will be transferred to and operated by Musarubra Korea Limited with an anticipated date of June 2, 2022.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">As a result of this transfer, personal information will be transferred to Musarubra Korea Limited. For more details. please click <a href="/content/dam/consumer/en-us/docs/legal/public-notice-for-personal-information-transfer-korea.pdf" target="_blank">here</a> for the public notice on the transfer of personal information.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="links"></a>Links to Other Websites</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Our Site and Services may contain links to other websites for your convenience and information. These websites may be operated by companies not affiliated with McAfee. Linked websites may have their own privacy policies or notices, which we strongly suggest you review if you visit those websites. We are not responsible for the content, privacy practices, or use of any websites that are not affiliated with McAfee.</span></p>

<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Click <a href="/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/privacy-contact.html">here</a> to contact us regarding this Privacy Notice or other related Privacy issues. You can also write to us as follows:</span></p>

<div class="cmp-text cmp__richtext--color cmp__richtext--color-null" v-if="validateDigitalRule('')">
<h2 style="text-align: center;">Cookie Notice</h2>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cmp-divider aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><hr/></div>
<div class="richtext text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text cmp__richtext--color cmp__richtext--color-null" v-if="validateDigitalRule('')">
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Effective date: May 24, 2018</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Our websites and mobile apps (collectively, the “Services”) use cookies and similar technologies to ensure that we give our visitors the best possible experience by providing you personalized information, remembering your marketing and product preferences, and helping you obtain the right information. This Notice describes how McAfee, our affiliates, and our partners use cookies and similar technologies for these purposes.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">What Technologies Does McAfee and Its Partners Use?</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Like many services, we and our partners use cookies and similar technologies to do things like provide and improve your experience and to customize advertising. The cookies and similar technologies we and our partners use include the following:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Cookies. Cookies are small files—usually consisting of letters and numbers—placed on your browser or device when you visit a website. Cookies are widely used to help facilitate the operation of websites, to help them work more efficiently, and to provide analytic information.<br/>
<br/>
</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"> SDKs. SDKs are blocks of code provided by our partners that may be installed in our mobile applications. SDKs help us understand how you interact with our mobile applications and collect certain information about the device and network you use to access the application or the other applications installed on your device. SDKs often share the mobile advertising identifier assigned to your device (called “IDFA” or “ID for Advertising” on Apple devices and “Advertising ID” on Android devices) with our partners.<br/>
<br/>
</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Flash Cookies. A Flash Cookie is a small data file placed on a computer using Adobe Flash or similar technology that may be built into your computer or downloaded or installed by you to your computer. We use these technologies to personalize and enhance your online experience, facilitate processes, and personalize and store your settings. Flash cookies may help our website visitors to, for example, set volume preference associated with a video experience, play games, and perform surveys. They help us improve our sites by measuring which areas are of greatest interest to guests. <a href="http://www.macromedia.com/support/documentation/en/flashplayer/help/settings_manager03.html" target="_blank"><u>Click here</u></a> to learn how to manage privacy and storage settings for Flash cookies.<br/>
<br/>
</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Web Beacons. A web beacon is a very small clear picture file used to keep track of your navigation through a single website or a series of websites. They may also be referred to as “web bugs” or “clear gifs.” Web beacons may be used with cookies to gain an understanding of how a website’s users navigate through the website.<br/>
<br/>
</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Local Storage. Local storage includes HTML5 local storage and browser cache. These technologies allow us to store data locally on your browser or device.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">McAfee and its partners and service providers use different types of cookies, as follows:</span></p>
</div>

<th scope="col"><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Category</span></th>
<th scope="col"><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Purpose</span></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Essential
</span></th>
<td><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">These cookies are required for the operation of our Services (for example, to enable you to log into secure areas of our website or use a shopping cart). These cookies enable you to move around the Services and use their features.</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Customization</span></th>
<td><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">These Cookies are used to recognize you when you return to our Services. This enables us to personalize content for you, greet you by name, and remember your preferences (for example, your choice of language or region).
</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Analytics and Research
</span></th>
<td><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">These cookies allow us to analyze activities on our Services in order to improve and optimize the way our Services work. For example, we may use these cookies to ensure that visitors can easily find the information they are looking for.
</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<th scope="row"><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Advertising</span></th>
<td><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">These cookies record your online activities, including your visits to our Services, the pages you have visited, and the links and advertisements you have clicked. These cookies allow us to deliver advertisements and other communications to you that are more relevant to your interests.
</span></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="richtext text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text cmp__richtext--color cmp__richtext--color-null" v-if="validateDigitalRule('')">
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">What Are My Choices with Respect to Cookies and Similar Technologies?</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">You have a variety of choices with respect to the use of cookies and similar technologies:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">You can decide whether or not to accept cookies by using your browser's settings. You may also be able to remove cookies from your browser. For more information about how to manage browser cookies, please follow the instructions provided by your browser. Please note that if you block all cookies, it may affect the functionality of our websites.<br/>
<br/>
</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">The advertising technology partners with which we partner may provide you the option to opt out of the use of information about your website visits and app usage for purposes of serving ads that are targeted to your interests. You can learn more about interest-based advertising and how to opt out of the use of your web browsing activity for interest-based advertising purposes by visiting these sites: <a href="http://www.aboutads.info/"><u>Digital Advertising Alliance</u></a>, the <a href="https://www.networkadvertising.org/"><u>Network Advertising Initiative</u></a>, and the <a href="https://iabeurope.eu/"><u>Interactive Advertising Bureau (IAB) Europe</u></a>.<br/>
<br/>
</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">You may opt out of the use of information about your mobile app usage for purposes of serving ads that are targeted to your interests through your device settings (called “Limit Ad Tracking” on iOS devices and “Opt Out of Interest-Based Advertising” or “Opt Out of Ads Personalization” on Android devices).<br/>
<br/>
</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Certain McAfee products are made available for free. In order to keep these products free, we may use information about websites you visit or the mobile applications you use to show you ads that are targeted to your interests. We do this by sharing information about your device—such as your device and advertising identifiers, together with web browsing activity or app usage—with select partners. This information does not identify you personally and we contractually prohibit the partners from using the information we provided to attempt to identify our users. You can opt out of the use of your information for this purpose in the settings of the products that include this data sharing. You can learn more about the options available to you for particular products and services by clicking <a href="https://service.mcafee.com/webcenter/portal/oracle/webcenter/page/scopedMD/s55728c97_466d_4ddb_952d_05484ea932c6/Page29.jspx?platform=&amp;showFooter=false&amp;locale=en-US&amp;fromSearch=true&amp;articleId=TS102592&amp;leftWidth=0%25&amp;showHeader=false&amp;wc.contextURL=%2Fspaces%2Fcp&amp;rightWidth=0%25¢erWidth=100%25&amp;_adf.ctrl-state=sgtjj1zg9_9&amp;_afrLoop=23477124777652#!"><u>here</u></a>.<br/>
<br/>
</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Finally, we participate with the Facebook Audience Network, which provides a way for companies to display their ads to Facebook users in apps and websites that are also part of the network. Facebook helps tailor the ads so that they are relevant and useful. You can use Facebook's ad preferences tool to view and change your preferences, including whether you receive these tailored ads, on our website and apps.<br/>
  </span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">How Does McAfee respond to a Do Not Track Signal?</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">There is currently no industry agreed upon response to a Do Not Track signal. At this time, McAfee Services and Sites do not respond to a user's Do Not Track signal.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">How to Contact Us</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you have any questions about how we use cookies and similar technologies, you can contact us using the information below. Please include your contact information and a detailed description of your concern.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">In the United States by calling us at +1 866 622 3911 or by writing to us at:</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Attn: Legal Department – Privacy Office <br/>

<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">In the European Economic Area by calling us at +353 21 467 2000 or by writing to us at:</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">McAfee, Legal Department<br/>

<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">You have the right to make a complaint at any time to the Data Protection Commissioner, the Irish supervisory authority for data protection issues, at <a href="https://www.dataprotection.ie/"><u>https://www.dataprotection.ie/docs/Home/4.htm</u></a>, or by calling +353 57 868 4800.</span></p>

<section class="main__section main__section--default aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

<div class="main__section--wrapper-container">

<div class="col section__container__col">
<article class="responsivegrid">
<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12">
<div class="cmp-sectioncontent aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text cmp__richtext--color cmp__richtext--color-default" v-if="validateDigitalRule('')">
<h2 style="text-align: center;">Privacy Notice for McAfee® WebAdvisor (Mozilla)</h2>
</div>
</div>
<div class="cmp-divider aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><hr/></div>
<div class="richtext text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
<div class="cmp-text cmp__richtext--color cmp__richtext--color-default" v-if="validateDigitalRule('')">
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Effective date: December 01, 2021</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">This Notice provides information about data we collect, use, and share, and our commitment to using the personal data we collect in a respectful fashion.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We at McAfee, LLC, including our affiliates (“McAfee”, “we”, “us”, “our”), care deeply about privacy, security, and online safety, all of which are a significant part of our essential mission: to protect users of our products and services (“you” and “your”) from the risks of theft, disruption, and unauthorized access to their online information and activities. This Privacy Notice (“Notice”) is designed to inform you about how we collect, use, and share your personal data through the McAfee® WebAdvisor extension that you downloaded for your Firefox Browser ("WebAdvisor" or the “Services”) or when you interact with us.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">When you access or use our Services, you acknowledge that you have read this Notice and understand its contents. Your use of our Services and any dispute over privacy is subject to this Notice, any applicable Terms of Service (including any applicable limitations on damages and the resolution of disputes) and any applicable End User License Agreement.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">As McAfee grows, our business changes, and we may update this Notice at any time as we deem appropriate to reflect those changes. If there are any material changes to this Privacy Notice, we will notify you by email, in-product notification, or as otherwise required by applicable law. It is important that you check back and make sure that you have reviewed the most current version of this Notice.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">This Notice applies to all users of our Services across the world. Some users, including residents of the European Economic Area, may have additional rights depending on where they are located, which are described in this Notice.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="information"></a>What Kinds of Information Do We Collect?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">In order to provide our services, we collect information. Some information you provide directly to us, some we collect automatically through our Services. In this Notice, "Personal Data" refers to data that could be used, alone or in combination with other data, to identify you as an individual.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>We collect information you provide to us</b>. We collect your contact information (such as name, email address, and phone number) if you choose to fill out a form or survey, request customer service, or otherwise communicate with us.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">You may also provide us with additional data. For example, when you use our identity monitoring services, you will have the option to provide your social media log-in information so that we can monitor your social media accounts.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>We automatically collect information about your interactions with the Services as well as devices on which the Services are installed. </b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">For example, we may collect and use the following:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Details about your computers, devices, applications, and networks, including internet protocol (IP) address, device IDs, and other device identifiers that are automatically assigned to your computer or device when you access the Internet, browser type and language, language preferences, hardware type, operating system, pages that you visit before and after using the Services and, in some cases, the date and time of your visit, and other actions taken through use of the Services such as preferences. </span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Details about your internet, app, or network usage (including URLs or domain names of websites you visit, or traffic data); and performance information, crash logs, and other aggregate or statistical information.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">In order to provide you our Services, including to detect and evaluate malware and spam, we may scan, collect, and store URLs and traffic data, as well as metadata about files downloaded from the Internet, such as name and size.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="how"></a>How Do We Use the Information We Collect?</b></span><br/>
</p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>To Help Protect You</b><br/>
 When you install or use our Services, it will run in the background of your device or environment to help predict threats and better protect you, your devices, and your information. For example, McAfee may use information to:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Analyze data sent to/from your device(s) to isolate and identify threats, vulnerabilities, viruses, suspicious activity, spam, and attacks, and communicate with you about potential threats;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Participate in threat intelligence networks, conduct research, and adapt products and services to help respond to new threats;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Check for Service updates and create performance reports on our Services, to ensure they are performing properly; and</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>To Run Our Business<br/>
</b>We also use the information we collect for other business purposes, including to:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Analyze your behavior to measure, customize, and improve our Site and Services, including developing new products and services;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Advertise McAfee products and services that we think may be of interest to you;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Provide customer support, troubleshoot issues, and respond to requests, questions, and comments;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Communicate about, and administer participation in, special events, programs, surveys, contests, sweepstakes, and other offers and promotions;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Conduct market and consumer research and trend analyses;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Enable posting on our blogs, forums, and other public communications;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Prevent, detect, identify, investigate, and respond to potential or actual claims, liabilities, prohibited behavior, and criminal activity; and</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Comply with and enforce legal rights, requirements, agreements, and policies.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="third"></a>Third-Party Advertising</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We work with third-party advertising companies to display or deliver ads to you while you are on our Site or using some Services. These third-party advertisers may collect data about your interaction with the Site or Services or others’ sites or services to measure the effectiveness of their ads and to personalize advertising content. See our <a href="#cookie" target="_blank"><u>Cookie Notice</u></a> to learn more about how McAfee and these advertising partners use tracking technologies like cookies and the choices available to you.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="who"></a>Who Do We Share Personal Data With?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Generally, we disclose the information we collect to provide the Services, to communicate with you, to advertise or promote our Services, to facilitate changes to or transfers of our business, as required by law, or with your consent. We may share Personal information in the following ways:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">With current and future members of the McAfee family of companies for the purposes described in this Notice;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">With service providers who perform services for us (the list of our sub-processors for <u><a href="/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html" target="_blank">Consumer Products</a></u> is available upon request for where required under applicable laws)</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If we believe disclosure is necessary and appropriate to prevent physical, financial, or other harm, injury, or loss, including to protect against fraud or credit risk;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">To legal, governmental, or judicial authorities as instructed or required by those authorities and applicable laws, or in relation to a legal activity, such as in response to a subpoena or investigation of suspected illicit or illegal activities, or where we believe in good faith that users may be engaged in illicit or illegal activities, or where we are bound by contract or law to enable a customer or business partner to comply with applicable laws;</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">In connection with, or during negotiations for, an acquisition, merger, asset sale, or other similar business transfer that involves all or substantially all of our assets or functions where Personal Data is transferred or shared as part of the business assets (provided that such party agrees to use or disclose such Personal Data consistent with this Notice or gains your consent for other uses or disclosures);</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">With your consent or at your direction, such as when you choose to share information or publicly post content and reviews (for example, social media posts); and</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">With persons of your choosing and at your discretion, should the product you are subscribed to allow that functionality.</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We may also share aggregate data that does not identify you or any specific device with third parties.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="security"></a>How Do We Protect Your Data?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We use administrative, organizational, technical, and physical safeguards to protect the Personal Data we collect and process. Our security controls are designed to maintain data confidentiality, integrity, and an appropriate level of availability.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="choices"></a>What Choices Do You Have About Your Personal Data?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><span><b>Individual Rights in Personal Data</b><br/>
 In accordance with applicable law, you may have the right to: (i) request confirmation of whether we are processing your Personal Data; (ii) obtain access to or a copy of your Personal Data; (iii) receive a portable copy of your Personal Data, or ask us to send that information to another organization (the “right of data portability”); (iv) seek correction or amendment of inaccurate, untrue, incomplete, or improperly processed Personal Data; (v) restrict our processing of your Personal Data; (vi) object to our processing of your Personal Data; and (vii) request erasure of Personal Data held about you by us, subject to certain exceptions prescribed by law.</span></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you would like to exercise any of these rights, please visit our Individual Data Request Form available at <a href="/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html">https://www.mcafee.com/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html</a> or contact us as set forth below. We will process such requests in accordance with applicable laws. To protect your privacy, we may take steps to verify your identity before fulfilling your request. For some requests and where permitted by law, an administrative fee may be charged. We will advise you of any applicable fee prior to performing your request.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="retain"></a>How Long Does McAfee Retain the Personal Data it Collects?</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">McAfee will keep your Personal Data for the minimum period necessary for the purposes set out in this Notice, namely (i) for as long as you are a registered subscriber or user of our products or (ii) for as long as your Personal Data are necessary in connection with the lawful purposes set out in this Notice, for which we have a valid legal basis or (iii) for as long as is reasonably necessary for business purposes related to provision of the Services, such as internal reporting and reconciliation purposes, warranties or to provide you with feedback or information you might request. Where required by law, we will delete your biometric data within three years of your last interaction with the Services.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">In addition, if any relevant legal claims are brought, we may continue to process your Personal Data for such additional periods as are necessary in connection with that claim.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Once the abovementioned periods, each to the extent applicable, have concluded, we will either permanently delete, destroy, or de-identify the relevant Personal Data so that it can no longer reasonably be tied to you.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="childrens"></a>Children's Privacy</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Some of McAfee’s products provide security features that parents may use to monitor their child’s activity online, physical location, or use of a registered device. WebAdvisor is not one of these products. If you are under the age of 18, you must have your parent’s permission to access the Services. McAfee urges parents to instruct their children never to give out their real names, addresses, or phone numbers, without parental permission. If you learn that your child has provided us with Personal Data without your consent, you may alert us by contacting us as described below. If we learn that we have collected any Personal Data from children under 13 (and in certain jurisdictions under the age of 16), we will promptly take steps to delete such information and terminate the child’s account.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Data Transfers</b><br/>
 McAfee is headquartered in the United States (see Contact Us for addresses), and we have operations, entities, and service providers in the United States and throughout the world. As such, we and our service providers may transfer your Personal Data to, or store or access it in, jurisdictions that may not provide equivalent levels of data protection as your home jurisdiction. We will take steps to ensure that your Personal Data receives an adequate level of protection in the jurisdictions in which we process it.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="eea"></a>Residents of the European Economic Area</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you are in the European Economic (EEA), the following additional disclosures apply.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Data Controller</b><br/>
 Where you purchase or download one of McAfee’s consumer products, McAfee Ireland Limited acts as the Controller of your Personal Data.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Legal Basis for Processing</b><br/>
 When we process your Personal Data, we will only do so in the following situations:</span></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We need to use your Personal Data to perform our responsibilities under our contract with you (e.g. processing payments for and providing the Services you purchase or request).</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We have a legitimate interest in processing your Personal Data. For example, we have a legitimate interest in processing your Personal Data to provide, secure, and improve our Services, in communicating with you about changes to our Services, and in informing you about new services or products.</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We have your consent to do so.</span></li>
<li><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">We need to process your Personal Data to comply with our legal obligations.</span></li>
</ul>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Data Transfers</b><br/>
 We transfer Personal Data to countries outside of the EEA or Switzerland through a series of intercompany agreements based on the Standard Contractual Clauses in accordance with EU law and applicable EU regulations.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Individual Rights Requests and Withdraw Consent</b><br/>
 You may submit a request to exercise your rights in Personal Data using the mechanisms explained under "What Choices Do You Have About Your Personal Data?" above. If you initially consented to our processing of your Personal Data, you may withdraw your consent using those mechanisms or by contacting us using the contact information below.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="authority"></a>Supervisory Authority and Complaints</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you are an EU/EEA Data Subject and have a concern about our practices concerning the processing of Personal Data that we are not able to resolve, you have the right to lodge a complaint with the data protection authority where you reside or in which you work, or in which the alleged infringement occurred, each as applicable, or by contacting the Irish supervisory authority for data protection issues, at <a href="https://www.dataprotection.ie/docs/Home/4.htm">https://www.dataprotection.ie/docs/Home/4.htm</a>, or +353 57 868 4800.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="japan"></a>Residents of Japan, Argentina, and Canada</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you are a resident of Japan, Argentina, or Canada and you have an inquiry regarding your personal information held by McAfee, including your personal information collected through your use of our products you may request further information using the Individual Data Request Form available at <a href="/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html">https://www.mcafee.com/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html</a>.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="california"></a>Residents of California</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><b>Your California Privacy Rights - Shine the Light Law</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">McAfee does not share information that identifies you personally with non-affiliated third parties for their own marketing use without your permission.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black"><a><b>California Consumer Privacy Act</b></a></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">If you are a resident of California, you may submit a request to exercise your rights in Personal Data using the Individual Data Request Form available at <a href="/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html">https://www.mcafee.com/en-us/consumer-support/policy/legal/gdpr-data-request.html</a> For purposes of the California Consumer Privacy Act, McAfee does not “sell” your Personal Data.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="nevada"></a>Residents of Nevada</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">McAfee does not sell information that identifies you personally with non-affiliated third parties. If you would like to make a request that we not sell identifying information about you in the future, you may make a request using the contact information below.</span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-md"><b><a id="links"></a>Links to Other Websites</b></span></p>
<p><span class="font-size-sm-m rteFontColor font-color-black">Our Site and Services may contain links to other websites for your convenience and information. These websites may be operated by companies not affiliated with McAfee. Linked websites may have their own privacy policies or notices, which we strongly suggest you review if you visit those websites. We are not responsible for the content, privacy practices, or use of any websites that are not affiliated with McAfee.</span></p>
